type Unmarked;\n    fn mark(unmarked: Self::Unmarked) -> Self;\n}\n\n/// Unwrap types wrapped by `Mark::mark` (see `Mark` for details).\ntrait Unmark {\n    type Unmarked;\n    fn unmark(self) ->
